<head>
<title>5.2 Selector Syntax</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
.cl1:first-line strong {color: red;}
.cl2em {color: red;}
.cl2+.cl3 {color: green;}
.cl3  +  .cl4 {color: green;}</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 5.2 Selector Syntax</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="index.html">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-02-01.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#q2">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>.cl1:first-line strong {color: red;}
.cl2em {color: red;}
.cl2+.cl3 {color: green;}
.cl3  +  .cl4 {color: green;}
</pre>
<hr>
<p class="cl1">
[cl1] The <em>emphasized text</em> in the first line of this element should NOT be red, but the same color as the text in the element.
</p>
<p class="cl2">
[cl2] The <em>emphasized text</em> in this element should NOT be red, but the same color as the text in the element.
</p>
<p class="cl3">
[cl3] The text in this element should be green.
</p>
<p class="cl4">
[cl4] The text in this element should be green.
</p>
<hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="index.html">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-02-01.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#q2">Specification</A>]
<HR>
</body>

<head>
<title>5.2.1 Grouping</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
.cl1, .cl2, .cl3 {color: green;}
.cl4, %cl5 {color: red;}</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 5.2.1 Grouping</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-02.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-03.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#grouping">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>.cl1, .cl2, .cl3 {color: green;}
.cl4, %cl5 {color: red;}
</pre>
<hr>
<P class="cl1">
[cl1] This sentence should be green.
</P>
<P class="cl2">
[cl2] This sentence should be green.
</P>
<P class="cl3">
[cl3] This sentence should be green.
</P>
<P class="cl4">
[cl4] This sentence should be black.
</P>
<P class="cl5">
[cl5] This sentence should be black.
</P>
<hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-02.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-03.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#grouping">Specification</A>]

##### sec05-03.htm #####
<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/html4/loose.dtd"> 
<html>
<head>
<title>5.3 Universal Selector</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
* {text-decoration: overline;}
*.cl1 {color: purple;}
.pastoral {color: green;}  /* omitted universal selector should be inferred */
big {font-size: 133%; color: rgb(60%,60%,40%);}
</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 5.3 Universal Selector</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-02-01.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-04.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#universal-selector">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>* {text-decoration: overline;}
*.cl1 {color: purple;}
.pastoral {color: green;}  /* omitted universal selector should be inferred */
big {font-size: 133%; color: rgb(60%,60%,40%);}

</pre>
<hr>
<P>
This is a paragraph element, which should be overlined.  In fact, <big>all</big> of the elements on this page should be overlined.  The word "all" in this paragraph may therefore appear to have two overlines, one consistent with the normal text and one slightly higher than that.  (Other renderings may be possible.)  However, the overline for the <code>big</code> element should be a dusky yellow no matter where it appears.
</P>
<UL>
<LI>The list items in this list...</LI>
<LI>...should be black, except for...
<LI class="cl1">...this item, which should be purple [cl1]...</LI>
<LI>...and this should be black again.</LI>
</UL>
<H3>This H3 should be black.</H3>
<H4 class="cl1">This H4 should be purple. [cl1]</H4>

<HR>

<H3 class="pastoral">[pastoral] An H3 element which should be green.</H1>
<P class="pastoral">[pastoral] A paragraph element which should be green.</P>
<blockquote class="pastoral">[pastoral] A blockquote element which should be green.</blockquote>
<PRE class="pastoral">[pastoral] A PRE element which should be green.</PRE>
<hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-02-01.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-04.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#universal-selector">Specification</A>]
<HR>
</body>
</html>

<head>
<title>5.4 Type Selectors</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
H1 {font-family: sans-serif;}
BODY {color: purple;}
P {color: green;}
H3 {color: navy;}
LI {color: green;}</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 5.4 Type Selectors</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-03.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-05.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#type-selectors">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>H1 {font-family: sans-serif;}
BODY {color: purple;}
P {color: green;}
H3 {color: navy;}
LI {color: green;}
</pre>
<hr>
<H1>This H1 should be sans-serif.</H1>
<P>
This paragraph should be green.
</P>
<P class="tester">This paragraph should be green despite having a class of 'tester'.</P>
<H3>This H3 should be navy (dark blue).</H3>
<UL>
<LI>This list item should be green...</LI>
<LI>...as should this.</LI>
</UL>
<OL>
<LI>This list item should be green...</LI>
<LI>...as should this.</LI>
</OL>
<H5>This H5 should be purple.</H5>
<P>
Another paragraph o' green.
</P><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-03.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-05.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#type-selectors">Specification</A>]

</body>

##### sec05-05.htm #####
<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/html4/loose.dtd"> 
<html>
<head>
<title>5.5 Descendant Selectors</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
H1 EM {color: blue;}
P STRONG {color: maroon;}
DIV * P {color: green;}
LI * STRONG {color: green;}</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 5.5 Descendant Selectors</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-04.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-06.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#descendant-selectors">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>H1 EM {color: blue;}
P STRONG {color: maroon;}
DIV * P {color: green;}
LI * STRONG {color: green;}
</pre>
<hr>
<H1>This <SPAN class="myclass">headline is <EM>very</EM> important</SPAN></H1>
<P>The EM text in the previous H1 element should be blue.</P>

<HR>

<P>
The strongly emphasized text in this paragraph should be <STRONG>maroon</STRONG>.
</P>
<P>
The strongly emphasized text in this paragraph <EM>should be <STRONG>maroon</STRONG></EM>, despite being the child of an EM element.
</P>
<P>
In this paragraph we have an anchor which contains emphasized text, which in turn contains a citation, which in turn contains strongly emphasized text-- and that text should be maroon.  Here goes: <A HREF="http://www.w3.org/">The W3C Web site contains a <EM>great resource called <CITE>The CSS2 <STRONG>Test Suite</STRONG></CITE> (if we do say so ourselves)</EM>.</A>
</P>

<HR>

<DIV>
This is anonymous text within a DIV, followed by:
<DIV>
...another DIV, with more anonymous text, followed by:
<P>...a paragraph, which should be green in color.</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>

<HR>

<UL>
<LI>This STRONG text in this list...</LI>
<LI>should <STRONG>not be green</STRONG>, as it is a child of the LI element.</LI>
</UL>
<UL>
<LI>This STRONG text in this list...</LI>
<LI><EM>should <STRONG>be green</STRONG>, as it is a grandchild of the LI element</EM>.</LI>
</UL>
<hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-04.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-06.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#descendant-selectors">Specification</A>]
<HR>
</body>
</html>
##### sec05-06.htm #####
<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/html4/loose.dtd"> 
<html>
<head>
<title>5.6 Child Selectors</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
BODY > P {color: green;}
BODY>P.cl1 {font-family: sans-serif;}
DIV OL > LI STRONG {color: green;}</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 5.6 Child Selectors</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-05.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-07.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#child-selectors">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>BODY &gt; P {color: green;}
BODY&gt;P.cl1 {font-family: sans-serif;}
DIV OL &gt; LI STRONG {color: green;}
</pre>
<hr>
<P>
This paragraph, as a direct child of the BODY, should be green.
</P>
<P class="cl1">
[cl1] This paragraph, as a direct child of the BODY and bearing a class of 'cl1', should be green and in a sans-serif font.
</P>
<DIV>
<P>
This paragraph, which is a child of a DIV, should NOT be green.
</P>
<UL>
<LI>The STRONG text in this list...</LI>
<LI>...should <STRONG>not be green</STRONG>, since it is part of an unordered list.</LI>
</UL>
<OL>
<LI>The STRONG text in this list...</LI>
<LI>...should <STRONG>be green</STRONG>, since it is a descendant of an LI which is a child of an OL element that's a descendant of the BODY.</LI>
<LI>This item contains an unordered list:
<UL>
<LI>The STRONG text in this list...</LI>
<LI>...should <STRONG>be green</STRONG>, since it is also a descendant of an LI which is a child of an OL element that's a descendant of the BODY.</LI>
</UL>
</LI>
<LI>One more list item, just for good measure, containing <STRONG>strongly empahsized text</STRONG> which should be green.
</OL>
</DIV><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-05.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-07.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#child-selectors">Specification</A>]
<HR>
</body>
</html>
##### sec05-07.htm #####
<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/html4/loose.dtd"> 
<html>
<head>
<title>5.7 Adjacent Sibling Selectors</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
H3 + H4 {color: green;}
UL+P {border-top: 3px solid green;}  /* lack of whitespace shouldn't matter */
EM + STRONG {color: green;}
H3.opener + P {border-top: 3px solid green;}</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 5.7 Adjacent Sibling Selectors</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-06.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-08-01.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#adjacent-selectors">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>H3 + H4 {color: green;}
UL+P {border-top: 3px solid green;}  /* lack of whitespace shouldn't matter */
EM + STRONG {color: green;}
H3.opener + P {border-top: 3px solid green;}
</pre>
<hr>
<H3>Here's an H3 element</H3>
<H4>This H4 should be green</H4>

<HR>

<H3>Here's another H3 element</H3>
this text is not in an element, and so shouldn't affect the adjacency selector; thus:
<H4>This H4 should be green</H4>

<HR>

<H3>Here's another H3 element</H3>
<P>This text is contained within a paragraph element, and so should affect the adjacency selector; thus:</P>
<H4>This H4 should NOT be green</H4>

<HR>

<UL>
<LI>Look, it's an unordered list (no styles apply here).</LI>
</UL>
<P>
This paragraph, since it follows a UL element, should have a three-pixel green top border.
</P>
<P>
Within this paragraph, there is <EM>emphasized text which contains <STRONG>strongly emphasized text</STRONG> which should NOT be green</EM>, as well as <STRONG>strongly emphasized text</STRONG> which should be green.
</P>

<HR>

<H3 class="opener">This is an H3 with a class of "opener".</H3>
<P>
This paragraph should have a three-pixel solid green top border.
</P>
<P>
This paragraph should have no border.
</P><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-06.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-08-01.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#adjacent-selectors">Specification</A>]
<HR>
</body>
</html>
##### sec05-08-01.htm #####
<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/html4/loose.dtd"> 
<html>
<head>
<title>5.8.1 Attribute Selectors</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
P[class] {color: purple;}
P[class="one"] {color: green;}
P[class = "one"] {text-decoration: underline;}
P[class~="two"] {color: olive;}
P[class ~= "two"] {text-decoration: overline;}
P[class|="three"] {color: green;}
P[class |= "three"] {text-decoration: underline;}
P[class|="give"] {color: green;}
P[class~="give"][class~="generously"] {color: red;}
P[lang|="en"] {color: green;}
P[lang |= "de"] {color: green;}
A[HREF] {color: purple;}
A[HREF="http://www.erehwon.zzz/"] {color: green;}
A[NAME="hello"] {color: green;}
P[class="null"] {color: yellow; background: red; font-weight: bold;}
     /*  catch broken forward-compatible parsing */</STYLE>
</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 5.8.1 Attribute Selectors</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-07.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-08-03.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#attribute-selectors">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>P[class] {color: purple;}
P[class="one"] {color: green;}
P[class = "one"] {text-decoration: underline;}
P[class~="two"] {color: olive;}
P[class ~= "two"] {text-decoration: overline;}
P[class|="three"] {color: green;}
P[class |= "three"] {text-decoration: underline;}
P[class|="give"] {color: green;}
P[class~="give"][class~="generously"] {color: red;}
P[lang|="en"] {color: green;}
P[lang |= "de"] {color: green;}
A[HREF] {color: purple;}
A[HREF="http://www.erehwon.zzz/"] {color: green;}
A[NAME="hello"] {color: green;}
P[class="null"] {color: yellow; background: red; font-weight: bold;}
     /*  catch broken forward-compatible parsing */&lt;/STYLE&gt;

</pre>
<hr>
<P>
This is a paragraph, and should not be green.
</P>
<P class="test">
This is a paragraph with a class of 'test', and should be purple.
</P>
<P class="one">
This is a paragraph with a class of 'one', and should be green and underlined.
</P>
<P class="one step forward">
This is a paragraph with a class of 'one step forward', and should NOT be green (but purple instead), nor should it be underlined.
</P>
<P class="two steps back">
This is a paragraph with a class of 'two steps back', and should be olive and overlined.
</P>
<P class="one two three">
This is a paragraph with a class of 'one two three', and should be olive and overlined.
</P>
<P class="world war two">
This is a paragraph with a class of 'world war two', and should be olive and overlined.
</P>
<P class="three-blind-mice">
This is a paragraph with a class of 'three-blind-mice', and should be green and underlined.
</P>
<P class="bakers-three">
This is a paragraph with a class of 'bakers-three', and should NOT be green (but purple instead), nor should it be underlined.
</P>
<P class="give me liberty">
This is a paragraph with a class of 'give me liberty', and should be green.  If it is red, then it has inappropriately matched a rule which contains the classes 'give' and 'generously'; if it is black, it has not matched any attribute selector rules.  If it is purple, it has matched the attribute selector <code>[class]</code> but not any of the value-related selectors.
</P>
<P lang="en">
This is a paragraph with a LANG of 'en', and should be green.
</P>
<P lang="en-au">
This is a paragraph with a LANG of 'en-au', and should be green, mate.
</P>
<P lang="de-test">
This is a paragraph with a LANG of 'de-test', and should be green, ja?
</P>
<P>
The following hyperlinks should have the color indicated for each:
</P>
<UL>
<LI><A HREF="http://www.cwru.edu/">CWRU Web site</A> (purple)</LI>
<LI><A HREF="http://www.erehwon.zzz/">Mythical Web site</A> (green)</LI>
</UL>
<P>
The text between the dashes-- <A NAME="hello">you know, this stuff here</A>-- should be green, as it is contained by an anchor with a NAME of "hello".
</P><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-07.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-08-03.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#attribute-selectors">Specification</A>]
<HR>
</body>
</html>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 5.8.3 Class Selectors</h2>

</pre>

<P>A paragraph element which should NOT be green.</P>
<blockquote>A blockquote element which should NOT be green.</blockquote>
<PRE>A PRE element which should NOT be green.</PRE>

<HR>

<H3 class="pastoral">[pastoral] An H3 element which should be green.</H1>
<P class="pastoral">[pastoral] A paragraph element which should be green.</P>
<blockquote class="pastoral">[pastoral] A blockquote element which should be green.</blockquote>
<PRE class="pastoral">[pastoral] A PRE element which should be green.</PRE>

<H3 class="cl0">[cl0] An H3 element which should NOT be green.</H1>
<P class="cl0">[cl0] A paragraph which should be green.</P>
<blockquote class="cl0">[cl0] A blockquote element which should NOT be green.</blockquote>
<PRE class="cl0">[cl0] A PRE element which should NOT be green.</PRE>

<HR>

<P class="give me liberty">
This is a paragraph with a class of 'give me liberty', and should be red (border), white (background), and blue (foreground).
</P>

<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/html4/loose.dtd"> 
<html>
<head>
<title>5.9 ID Selectors</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
#one {color: green;}
#1 {color: red;}
#id1 {color: green;}
P#id2 {color: blue;}
P#id3 {color: purple;}</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 5.9 ID Selectors</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-08-03.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-10.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#id-selectors">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>#one {color: green;}
#1 {color: red;}
#id1 {color: green;}
P#id2 {color: blue;}
P#id3 {color: purple;}
</pre>
<hr>
<P ID="one">
This sentence should be green.
</P>
<P ID="1">
[1] This sentence should be black, not red-- ID selectors cannot begin with digits in CSS1.
</P>
<P ID="id1">
[id1] This sentence should be green.
</P>
<P ID="id2">
[id2] This paragraph should be blue.
</P>
<PRE ID="id2">[id2] This sentence should NOT be blue.
</PRE>
<PRE ID="id3">[id3] This sentence should be black.
</PRE>
<UL>
<LI ID="id2">[id2] This sentence should NOT be blue.
<LI ID="id3">[id3] This sentence should NOT be purple.
</UL>
<P id="id11">
[id11] This paragraph should be black.
</P><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-08-03.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-10.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#id-selectors">Specification</A>]
<HR>
</body>
</html>

<html>
<head>
<title>5.11.1 :first-child</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
LI:first-child {color: green;}
P STRONG:first-child {color: green;}
DIV > P:first-child {color: purple;}
</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 5.11.1 :first-child</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-10.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-11-02.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#x25">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>LI:first-child {color: green;}
P STRONG:first-child {color: green;}
DIV &gt; P:first-child {color: purple;}

</pre>
<hr>
<UL>
<LI>This list item, being the first child of its parent, should be green.</LI>
<LI>This list item should NOT be green.
<OL>
<LI>Green list item</LI>
<LI>Non-green list item</LI>
<LI>Another non-green list item</LI>
</OL>
<LI>Still another non-green list item.</LI>
</UL>

<P>
The first child element of this paragraph is <STRONG>strongly emphasized text</STRONG>, and should be green, as is also the case for the <EM>strongly emphasized text which is <STRONG>the first child of the EM element</STRONG> found here.</EM>.  The <STRONG>STRONG text</STRONG> in this sentence should NOT be green, since it is not the first child of anything.
</P>
<P>
In this paragraph, we have some <EM>emphasized text</EM>, and then a little later, some <STRONG>strongly emphasized text</STRONG>, which should NOT be green, since it is the second child of the paragraph (the EM element is the first).
</P>

<HR>

<DIV>
Within this DIV...
<P>There is a paragraph, and as the first child, it should be purple.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV>
Within this DIV...
<H3>An H3 element</H3>
<P>There is a paragraph, and as the second child, it should NOT be either purple or green.</P>
<UL>
<LI>Within this unordered list, there is a paragraph which is the first child of a list item.</LI>
<LI>The paragraph, where starts here:
<P>should NOT be purple, since it is not the first-child of a DIV.</P>
...and there you have it.</LI>
</UL>
</DIV>
<hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-10.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-11-02.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#x25">Specification</A>]
<HR>
</body>
</html>

A:link {color: purple;}
A:visited {color: lime;}
#id1 {color: #006600;}
A.external:link {color: olive;}
A.external:visited {color: maroon;}
</pre>

<UL>

<P>Dark green in any circumstance:</P>
<UL>
<LI><A HREF="http://www.cwru.edu/" ID="id1">[id1] CWRU Web server</A>
</UL>

<P>
The quoted word "<A NAME="test">anchor</A>" should be green, NOT purple, since it's part of an anchor.  It's a named anchor, and styles declared for the A tag are applied to them under CSS1.  It also should NOT turn orange when clicked upon.
</P>

<UL>
<LI><A HREF="http://www.3foo4bar5.com/" class="external">Unknown Web server [external]</A></LI>

<style type="text/css">
A {color: red;}
A:hover {color: cyan;}
A:active {color: maroon;}

A:focus:hover {color: lime;}

P.cl1:hover {background: yellow;}
TD:hover {background: silver;}
TD A:hover {color: red; background: yellow;}

INPUT:hover {background: yellow;}
INPUT:focus {background: #FF99FF;}
INPUT:focus:hover {background: #99FF99;}</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 5.11.3 :active, :hover, and :focus</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-11-02.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-11-04.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#x36">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>A {color: red;}
A:hover {color: cyan;}
A:active {color: maroon;}
A:focus {border: 1px solid red;}
A:focus:hover {color: lime;}

P.cl1:hover {background: yellow;}
TD:hover {background: silver;}
TD A:hover {color: red; background: yellow;}

INPUT:hover {background: yellow;}
INPUT:focus {background: #FF99FF;}
INPUT:focus:hover {background: #99FF99;}
</pre>
<hr>
<P>The following hyperlinks should become maroon (dark red) while active (being clicked), become cyan (light blue) while being hovered over but not in focus, have a one-pixel solid red border when in focus, and become lime (light green) when in focus and being hovered over:</P>

<UL>
<LI><A HREF="http://www.w3.org/">W3C Web server</A>
<LI><A HREF="http://www.nist.gov/">NIST Web server</A>
<LI><A HREF="http://www.cwru.edu/">CWRU Web server</A>
<LI><A HREF="http://www.yahoo.com/">Yahoo!</A>
<LI><A HREF="none.html">Erewhon</A> (don't click on it, it goes nowhere)
</UL>

<P>
This paragraph, and the one at the top of the page, should have no effects applied when the mouse pointer hovers over them.
</P>
<P class="cl1">
[cl1] This paragraph should attain a yellow background when the mouse pointer hovers over it, and have a transparent background in all other circumstances.  Extra text has been included in an attempt to have the paragraph display more than one line of text.
</P>
<TABLE border>
<TR>
<TD>This cell contains no anchor.</TD>
<TD>This cell <A HREF="http://www.w3.org/">contains</A> an anchor.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<HR>
<P>
The elements in the following form should have a yellow background when being hovered over, a purple background when in focus, and a light green background when in focus and being hovered over.
</P>
<FORM>
<P>
<INPUT type="text" name="inp1" size="30" value="Input 1"><BR>
<INPUT type="text" name="inp2" size="30" value="Input 2"><BR>
<INPUT type="text" name="inp3" size="30" value="Input 3">
</P>
<P>
<INPUT type="radio" name="inp4" size="30">Input 4.1
<INPUT type="radio" name="inp4" size="30">Input 4.2
<INPUT type="radio" name="inp4" size="30">Input 4.3
</P>
</FORM><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-11-02.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-11-04.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#x36">Specification</A>]

<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/html4/loose.dtd">

<title>5.11.4 :lang</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
P:lang(en) {color: green;}
P:lang(de) {color: purple;}
</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 5.11.4 :lang</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-11-03.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-12-01.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#x42">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>P:lang(en) {color: green;}
P:lang(de) {color: purple;}

</pre>
<hr>
<div lang="et-kl">
<p>
This paragraph should NOT be any color except black.  It (along with all the test statements on this page) has an ancestor element with a <code>lang</code> attribute that has a value of <code>et-kl</code>, which is intended to reset any potentially inherited <code>lang</code> values, either from HTTP headers or the user's language settings.
</p>
<p lang="en">
[en] This paragraph has been marked English, and should be green.
</p>
<p lang="de">
[de] This paragraph has been marked Deutsch, despite the fact that it clearly is English, and should be purple.
</p>
<p lang="de-ch">
[de-ch] This paragraph has been marked as Swiss German, despite the fact that it clearly is English, and should be purple.
</p>
</div><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-11-03.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-12-01.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#x42">Specification</A>]
<HR>
</body>

<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/html4/loose.dtd"> 
<html>
<head>
<title>5.12.1 :first-line</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
P:first-line {color: green;}
.cl2:first-line {font-size: 200%;}
.cl3:first-line {font-variant: small-caps;}
</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 5.12.1 :first-line</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-11-04.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-12-02.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#first-line-pseudo">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>P:first-line {color: green;}
.cl2:first-line {font-size: 200%;}
.cl3:first-line {font-variant: small-caps;}

</pre>
<hr>
<P>
The first line of this paragraph, and only that one, should be green.  If this precise combination does not occur, then the user agent has failed this test.  Remember that in order to ensure a complete test, the paragraph must be displayed on more than one line.
</P>
<P class="cl2">
The first line of this paragraph, and only that one, should be a larger font size as well as green.  If this precise combination does not occur, then the user agent has failed this test.  Remember that in order to ensure a complete test, the paragraph must be displayed on more than one line. [cl2]
</P>
<P class="cl3">
The first line of this paragraph, and only that one, should be displayed in small-caps style.  Thus, if the first line is not in small-caps style, OR if the entire paragraph turns out in small-caps, then the user agent has failed this test (although the problem might be that <CODE>small-caps</CODE> is not supported by your browser).  This is extra text included for the purposes of making the paragraph long enough to have more than one line. [cl3]
</P>
<UL class="cl2">
<LI>The first line of this list item, and only this one, should be displayed with a <CODE>font-size</CODE> of <CODE>200%</CODE>.  Other lines in this list item should be at the normal size for this document.  This is extra text included for the purposes of making the list item long enough to have more than one line.  If it is not sufficient, please narrow your browser window in order to get the desired effect.</LI>
<LI>The first line of this list item should NOT be displayed with a <CODE>font-size</CODE> of <CODE>200%</CODE>.  Other lines in this list item should be at the normal size for this document.  This is extra text included for the purposes of making the list item long enough to have more than one line.  If it is not sufficient, please narrow your browser window in order to get the desired effect.</LI>
</UL><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-11-04.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-12-02.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#first-line-pseudo">Specification</A>]
<HR>
</body>
</html>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 5.12.2 :first-letter</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-12-01.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-12-03.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#x52">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>P:first-letter {color: maroon;}
.cl2:first-letter {font-size: 200%;}
P.cl3:first-letter {font-size: 350%;}

</pre>
<hr>
<P>
The first letter of this paragraph, and only that one, should be maroon.  If this precise combination does not occur, then the user agent has failed this test.  Remember that in order to ensure a complete test, the paragraph must be displayed on more than one line.
</P>
<P class="cl2">
The first letter of this paragraph, and only that one, should be a larger font size, as well as maroon.  If this precise combination does not occur, then the user agent has failed this test.  Remember that in order to ensure a complete test, the paragraph must be displayed on more than one line. [cl2]
</P>
<P class="cl3">
"We should check for quotation support," it was said.  The first two characters in this paragraph-- a double-quote mark and a capital 'W'-- should be 350% bigger than the rest of the paragraph, and maroon.  Note that this is not required under CSS1, but it is recommended. [cl3]
</P>
<UL class="cl2">
<LI>The first letter of this list item, and only this one, should be displayed with a <CODE>font-size</CODE> of <CODE>200%</CODE>.  Other letters in this list item should be at the normal size for this document.  This is extra text included for the purposes of making the list item long enough to have more than one line.  If it is not sufficient, please narrow your browser window in order to get the desired effect.</LI>
<LI>The first letter of this list item should NOT be displayed with a <CODE>font-size</CODE> of <CODE>200%</CODE>.  Other letters in this list item should be at the normal size for this document.  This is extra text included for the purposes of making the list item long enough to have more than one line.  If it is not sufficient, please narrow your browser window in order to get the desired effect.</LI>
</UL><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-12-01.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec05-12-03.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/selector.html#x52">Specification</A>]
<HR>
</body>
</html>

 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 5.12.3 :before and :after</h2>

<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>H3:before {content: "An H3 ";}
P.special:before {content: "Special! ";}
P.special:first-letter {color: green;}
P.special:after {content: " -- The End.";}
</pre>
<hr>
<H3>This H3 element should have generated content at its beginning.</H3>
<P>
This paragraph should have no generated content either before or after its content.
</P>
<P class="special">
This paragraph should start with the word "Special!" and the first letter "S" should be green.  Also, the paragraph should end with the words "The End." preceded by a double-dash composed of two hyphens.  That is all.
</P>

 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 6.2.1 inherit</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-12-03.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec06-03.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/cascade.html#value-def-inherit">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>P.cl1 {color: red;}
A:link {color: inherit; text-decoration: underline; font-weight: bold;}

</pre>
<hr>
<P class="cl1" style="color: inherit;">
[cl1] Although this paragraph has a class of 'cl1', it also has an inline STYLE of 'color: inherit', which should cause it to inherit its color from the BODY element.  Thus, the color should be black.
</P>
<P>
This unclassed <A HREF="http://www.w3.org/">paragraph</A> contains a number of <A HREF="http://www.cwru.edu/">anchors</A> which have been <A HREF="http://www.nist.gov/">underlined</A> and <A HREF="http://ech.cwru.edu/">boldfaced</A>, but whose <A HREF="http://www.cnn.com/">color</A> inherits from the paragraph itself (thus making them black).
</P><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec05-12-03.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec06-03.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/cascade.html#value-def-inherit">Specification</A>]

 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 6.3 @import</h2>

<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>@import "styleimport.css";
@import url(folder/styleimport.css);

/* This line resets any browsers that got confused by the @import lines */
.ignored { color: black; }

.style { font-weight: bold; color: green; background: silver none; }

<p>The style declaration applied in each following case is: <TT>{font-weight: bold; color: green; background: silver none;}</TT>.</P>

<p class="inline" style="font-weight: bold; color: green; background: silver none;">1. Inline style (<code>style</code> attribute).</p>
<p class="style">2. Embedded stylesheet (<code>style</code> element).</p>
<p class="styleimport">3. Stylesheet imported by embedded stylesheet.</p>
<p class="folderstyleimport">4. Stylesheet in another folder imported by embedded stylesheet.</p><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec06-02-01.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec06-04-01.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/cascade.html#at-import">Specification</A>]

<title>6.4.2 !important rules</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
P {color: green ! important;}
P {color: red;}
P#id1 {color: purple;}
</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 6.4.2 !important rules</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec06-04-01.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec06-04-03.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/cascade.html#important-rules">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>P {color: green ! important;}
P {color: red;}
P#id1 {color: purple;}

</pre>
<hr>
<P>
This sentence should be green, because the declaration marked important should override any other normal declaration for the same element, even if it occurs later in the stylesheet.
</P>
<P ID="id1">
[id1] This sentence should also be green, even though it has an ID of <TT>id1</TT>, which would ordinarily make it purple.  This is because declarations marked important have more weight than normal declarations given in a STYLE attribute.
</P>
<P style="color: red;">
This sentence should also be green, even though it has a STYLE attribute declaring it to be red.  This is because declarations marked important have more weight than normal declarations given in a STYLE attribute.
</P>
<hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec06-04-01.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec06-04-03.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/cascade.html#important-rules">Specification</A>]
<HR>
</body>

##### sec06-04-03.htm #####
<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/html4/loose.dtd"> 
<html>
<head>
<title>6.4.3 Calculating specificity</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
* {color: red;}  /* a=0 b=0 c=0 -> specificity =   0 */
LI  {color: maroon;}  /* a=0 b=0 c=1 -> specificity =   1 */
UL LI {color: green;}  /* a=0 b=0 c=2 -> specificity =   2 */
H1 + *[REL=up] {color: purple;}  /* a=0 b=1 c=1 -> specificity =  11 */
UL OL LI.olive {color: olive;}  /* a=0 b=1 c=3 -> specificity =  13 */ 
LI.olive.level {color: olive; font-weight: bold;}
   /* a=0 b=2 c=1 -> specificity =  21 */
#x34y {color: lime;}  /* a=1 b=0 c=0 -> specificity = 100 */ 


</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 6.4.3 Calculating specificity</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec06-04-02.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec06-04-04.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/cascade.html#specificity">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>* {color: red;}  /* a=0 b=0 c=0 -&gt; specificity =   0 */
LI  {color: maroon;}  /* a=0 b=0 c=1 -&gt; specificity =   1 */
UL LI {color: green;}  /* a=0 b=0 c=2 -&gt; specificity =   2 */
H1 + *[REL=up] {color: purple;}  /* a=0 b=1 c=1 -&gt; specificity =  11 */
UL OL LI.olive {color: olive;}  /* a=0 b=1 c=3 -&gt; specificity =  13 */ 
LI.olive.level {color: olive; font-weight: bold;}
   /* a=0 b=2 c=1 -&gt; specificity =  21 */
#x34y {color: lime;}  /* a=1 b=0 c=0 -&gt; specificity = 100 */ 



</pre>
<hr>
<P>
Although this unstyled paragraph, and many other elements on this page, may be red, this is acceptable.  For example, the text "No inheritance tests for this property" should be red.
</P>
<UL>
<LI>This list item should be green, not red (or any shade of it).</LI>
<LI>This similarly green list item contains an unordered list.
<OL>
<LI>This list item...</LI>
<LI>...and the ones following...</LI>
<LI>...should be green.</LI>
<LI class="olive">[olive] Not this, one, though; it should be a darker green.</LI>
<LI class="olive level two">[olive level two] This list item should be a darker green and boldfaced.</LI>
</OL>
</LI>
<LI>This list item should be green.</LI>
</UL>
<P ID="x34y">
[x34y] This paragraph should be lime.
</P>
<H1>An H1 element</H1>
<P rel="up">
[rel=up] This paragraph should be purple.
</P><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec06-04-02.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec06-04-04.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/cascade.html#specificity">Specification</A>]
<HR>
</body>

<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/html4/loose.dtd"> 
<html>
<head>
<title>6.4.4 Precedence of non-CSS hints</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
.cl1 {color: green;}</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 6.4.4 Precedence of non-CSS hints</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec06-04-03.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec08-02.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/cascade.html#q12">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>.cl1 {color: green;}
</pre>
<hr>
<P>
This paragraph contains text which is contained by <FONT class="cl1" color="red">[cl1] a FONT element with a color value of "red"</FONT>.  This should be overridden by the CSS rule for class 'cl1', which takes precedence over the non-CSS presentational hint embodied by the FONT element.  Therefore, the FONT-enclosed text should be green, not red.
</P><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec06-04-03.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec08-02.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/cascade.html#q12">Specification</A>]
<HR>
</body>

    border-style: dashed; border-width: medium;}
</style>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 8.2 Margins, padding, borders</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec06-04-04.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec08-03a.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/box.html#mpb-examples">Specification</A>]

<pre>ul {background: green;
    margin: 12px 12px 12px 12px;padding: 3px 3px 3px 3px;}

    margin: 12px 12px 12px 12px; padding: 12px 0px 12px 12px;
    list-style: none;}
li.withborder {border-color: black;
    border-style: dashed; border-width: medium;}

</pre>
<hr>
<ul>
<li>First element of list; there should be 12px of margin space between this list item and the next
<li class="withborder">Second element of list, which is much longer (in terms of content) in order to illustrate line wrapping and the effects of margins, padding, and borders in such a situation.  If your user agent's viewing area is too wide for this list item to be line-wrapped, please narrow the viewport until some line-wrapping is seen.
</ul>

 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 8.3 margin-bottom</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec08-03b.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec08-03d.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/box.html#propdef-margin-bottom">Specification</A>]

 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 8.3 margin </h2>

<div class="test">
[test] This 'div' element has no margins applied to it, and acts as a reference point.
</div>
<div class="test cl1">
[test cl1] This 'div' element should have an overall margin of 10 pixels.
</div>
<div class="test cl2">

</div>
<div class="test cl3">
[test cl3] This 'div' element should have an overall margin of 1em.
</div>
<div class="test cl4">
[test cl4] This 'div' element should have an overall margin of -2 pixels, and an aqua background.
</div>

</div>
<div class="test cl6">

</div>
<div class="test cl7">
[test cl7] This 'div' element should have margins of 10px top, 20px right, 10px bottom, and 20px left.
</div>
<div class="test">
[test] This 'div' element contains a 'span' element with a class of 'cl5' that should appear to have no top or bottom margins, but a 20px right margin and a -5px left margin.  If there is  <span class="cl5">[cl5]any increase of line separation</span> in the 'div' element due to the top and bottom margins on the 'span' element, the test has been failed; margins do not affect the height of lines.
</div><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec08-03d.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec08-04a.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/box.html#propdef-margin">Specification</A>]

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>
<div class="test cl4">

</div>

</div>

If there is  <span class="cl5">[cl5]any increase of line separation</span> in the 'div' element due to the top and bottom padding on the 'span' element, the test has been failed; padding does not affect the height of lines.  However, the padding may extend into or overlap other lines of text.

<html>
<head>
<title>8.5.1a border-top-width</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
.test {background-color: silver; border-style: solid; border-width: 0;}
.cl1 {border-top-width: thin;}
.cl2 {border-top-width: medium;}
.cl3 {border-top-width: thick;}
.cl4 {border-top-width: 5px;}
.cl5 {border-top-width: 0;}
.cl6 {border-top-width: -5px;}
</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 8.5.1 border-top-width</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec08-04e.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec08-05-01b.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/box.html#propdef-border-top-width">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>.test {background-color: silver; border-style: solid; border-width: 0;}
.cl1 {border-top-width: thin;}
.cl2 {border-top-width: medium;}
.cl3 {border-top-width: thick;}
.cl4 {border-top-width: 5px;}
.cl5 {border-top-width: 0;}
.cl6 {border-top-width: -5px;}

</pre>
<hr>
<p class="test">
[test] This 'p' element should have no border applied to it, as it has been given a zero-width overall border (this helps keep the following tests more clear).
</p>
<p class="test cl1">
[test cl1] This 'p' element should have a thin top border.
</p>
<p class="test cl2">
[test cl2] This 'p' element should have a medium top border.
</p>
<p class="test cl3">
[test cl3] This 'p' element should have a thick top border.
</p>
<p class="test cl4">
[test cl4] This 'p' element should have a 5px top border.
</p>
<p class="test cl5">
[test cl5] This 'p' element should have no top border.
</p>
<p class="test cl6">
[test cl6] This 'p' element should have no top border, as negative border widths are not permitted.
</p>
<p class="test">
[test] This 'p' element contains a 'span' element with a class of 'test cl4' that should have a 5px top border.  If there is <span class="test cl4">[test cl4]any increase of line separation</span> in the 'p' element due to the border on the 'span' element, the test has been failed; borders do not affect the height of lines.  However, the border may extend into or overlap other lines of text.
</p><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec08-04e.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec08-05-01b.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/box.html#propdef-border-top-width">Specification</A>]

However, the border may extend into or overlap other lines of text.

 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 8.5.1 border-bottom-width</h2>

.cl3 {border-bottom-width: thick;}
.cl4 {border-bottom-width: 5px;}
.cl5 {border-bottom-width: 0;}
.cl6 {border-bottom-width: -5px;}

</pre>
<hr>
<p class="test">
[test] This 'p' element should have no border applied to it, as it has been given a zero-width overall border (this helps keep the following tests more clear).
</p>
<p class="test cl1">
[test cl1] This 'p' element should have a thin bottom border.
</p>
<p class="test cl2">
[test cl2] This 'p' element should have a medium bottom border.
</p>
<p class="test cl3">
[test cl3] This 'p' element should have a thick bottom border.
</p>
<p class="test cl4">
[test cl4] This 'p' element should have a 5px bottom border.
</p>
<p class="test cl5">
[test cl5] This 'p' element should have no bottom border.
</p>
<p class="test cl6">
[test cl6] This 'p' element should have no bottom border, as negative border widths are not permitted.
</p>
<p class="test">
[test] This 'p' element contains a 'span' element with a class of 'test cl4' that should have a 5px bottom border.  If there is <span class="test cl4">[test cl4]any increase of line separation</span> in the 'p' element due to the border on the 'span' element, the test has been failed; borders do not affect the height of lines.  However, the border may extend into or overlap other lines of text.
</p><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec08-05-01b.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec08-05-01d.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/box.html#propdef-border-bottom-width">Specification</A>]

</pre>

[test] This 'p' element has no border width applied to it, and acts as a reference point.  It should default to the same border width as the result shown for 'medium' (cl2).
</p>

</p>

</p>
<p class="test cl6">
[test cl6] This 'p' element should have a default-width border, as negative border widths are not permitted.
</p>
<p class="test">
[test] This 'p' element contains a 'span' element with a class of 'test cl4' that should have a 5px overall border.  If there is  <span class="test cl4">[test cl4]any increase of line separation</span> in the 'p' element due to the border on the 'span' element, the test has been failed; borders do not affect the height of lines.  However, the border may extend into or overlap other lines of text.

</p>
<p class="test cl1">
[test cl1] This 'p' element should have a green top border, with the other border sides matching the text color.
</p>
<p class="test">
[test] This 'p' element contains a 'span' element with a class of 'test cl1' that should have a green top border and text-colored borders on the other sides.  If there is <span class="test cl1">[test cl1]any increase of line separation</span> in the 'p' element due to the border on the 'span' element, the test has been failed; borders do not affect the height of lines.  However, the border may extend into or overlap other lines of text.

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 8.5.3 border-top-style</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec08-05-02e.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec08-05-03b.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/box.html#propdef-border-top-style">Specification</A>]

<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>.test {background-color: silver; border-width: 5px; border-color: #753;}
.cl1 {border-top-style: solid;}
.cl2 {border-top-style: dotted;}
.cl3 {border-top-style: dashed;}
.cl4 {border-top-style: double;}
.cl5 {border-top-style: groove;}
.cl6 {border-top-style: ridge;}
.cl7 {border-top-style: inset;}
.cl8 {border-top-style: outset;}

</pre>
<hr>
<p class="test">
[test] This 'p' element should have no border applied to it, because its border style defaults to none.  The borders of 'test' elements in this test should be 5 pixels wide, and the color should be #753.
</p>
<p class="test cl1">
[test cl1] This 'p' element should have a solid top border.
</p>
<p class="test cl2">
[test cl2] This 'p' element should have a dotted top border.
</p>
<p class="test cl3">
[test cl3] This 'p' element should have a dashed top border.
</p>
<p class="test cl4">
[test cl4] This 'p' element should have a double top border.
</p>
<p class="test cl5">
[test cl5] This 'p' element should have a grooved top border.
</p>
<p class="test cl6">
[test cl6] This 'p' element should have a ridged top border.
</p>
<p class="test cl7">
[test cl7] This 'p' element should have an inset top border.
</p>
<p class="test cl8">
[test cl8] This 'p' element should have an outset top border.
</p>
<p class="test">
[test] This 'p' element contains a 'span' element with a class of 'cl1' that should have a solid top text-colored border.  If there is <span class="cl1">[cl1]any increase of line separation</span> in the 'p' element due to the border on the 'span' element, the test has been failed; borders do not affect the height of lines.  However, the border may extend into or overlap other lines of text.
</p><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec08-05-02e.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec08-05-03b.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/box.html#propdef-border-top-style">Specification</A>]

</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 8.5.3 border-right-style</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec08-05-03a.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec08-05-03c.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/box.html#propdef-border-right-style">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>.test {background-color: silver; border-width: 5px; border-color: #753;}
.cl1 {border-right-style: solid;}
.cl2 {border-right-style: dotted;}
.cl3 {border-right-style: dashed;}
.cl4 {border-right-style: double;}
.cl5 {border-right-style: groove;}
.cl6 {border-right-style: ridge;}
.cl7 {border-right-style: inset;}
.cl8 {border-right-style: outset;}

</pre>
<hr>
<p class="test">
[test] This 'p' element should have no border applied to it, because its border style defaults to none.  The borders of 'test' elements in this test should be 5 pixels wide, and the color should be #753.
</p>
<p class="test cl1">
[test cl1] This 'p' element should have a solid right border.
</p>
<p class="test cl2">
[test cl2] This 'p' element should have a dotted right border.
</p>
<p class="test cl3">
[test cl3] This 'p' element should have a dashed right border.
</p>
<p class="test cl4">
[test cl4] This 'p' element should have a double right border.
</p>
<p class="test cl5">
[test cl5] This 'p' element should have a grooved right border.
</p>
<p class="test cl6">
[test cl6] This 'p' element should have a ridged right border.
</p>
<p class="test cl7">
[test cl7] This 'p' element should have an inset right border.
</p>
<p class="test cl8">
[test cl8] This 'p' element should have an outset right border.
</p>
<p class="test">
[test] This 'p' element contains a 'span' element with a class of 'cl1' that should have a solid right text-colored border.  If there is <span class="cl1">[cl1]any increase of line separation</span> in the 'p' element due to the border on the 'span' element, the test has been failed; borders do not affect the height of lines.  However, the border may extend into or overlap other lines of text.
</p><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec08-05-03a.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec08-05-03c.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/box.html#propdef-border-right-style">Specification</A>]

.cl3 {border: 10px teal outset;}
.cl4 {border: 10px olive inset;}
.cl5 {border: 10px maroon;}
.cl6 {border: maroon double;}
.cl7 {border: left red solid;}
.cl8 {border: solid 0px;}</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 8.5.4 border </h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec08-05-04d.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec09-02-05.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/box.html#propdef-border">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>

.cl2 {border: thin maroon ridge;}
.cl3 {border: 10px teal outset;}
.cl4 {border: 10px olive inset;}
.cl5 {border: 10px maroon;}
.cl6 {border: maroon double;}
.cl7 {border: left red solid;}
.cl8 {border: solid 0px;}
</pre>
<hr>
<p class="test">
[test] This 'p' element should have no border applied to it, because its border style has been explicitly set to none.
</p>
<p class="test cl1">
[test cl1] This 'p' element should have an overall medium-width solid black border.
</p>
<p class="test cl2">
[test cl2] This 'p' element should have an overall thin ridged maroon border.
</p>
<p class="test cl3">
[test cl3] This 'p' element should have an overall 10px outset teal border.
</p>
<p class="test cl4">
[test cl4] This 'p' element should have an overall 10px inset olive border.
</p>
<p class="test cl5">
[test cl5] This 'p' element should have an overall 10 solid maroon border.
</p>
<p class="test cl6">
[test cl6] This 'p' element should have an overall medium-width double maroon border.
</p>
<p class="test cl7">
[test cl7] This 'p' element should have no border, as the value supplied is invalid.
</p>
<p class="test cl8">
[test cl8] This 'p' element should have no border, as its width has been set to zero.
</p>
<p class="test">
[test] This 'p' element contains a 'span' element with a class of 'cl1' that should have an overall medium-width solid black border.  If there is <span class="cl1">[cl1]any increase of line separation</span> in the 'p' element due to the border on the 'span' element, the test has been failed; borders do not affect the height of lines.  However, the border may extend into or overlap other lines of text.
</p><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec08-05-04d.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec09-02-05.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/box.html#propdef-border">Specification</A>]

<html>
<head>
<title>9.3.1 position</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
.cl1 {position: static; top: -5px; left: 2px;}
.cl2 {position: relative; top: -5px; left: 2px;}
.cl3 {position: absolute; top: 25px; left: 2px;}
.cl4 {position: fixed; top: 0px;  left: 200px;}
.contain {position: relative; background: yellow; height: 50px;}</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 9.3.1 position</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec09-02-05.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec09-03-02a.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/visuren.html#propdef-position">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>.cl1 {position: static; top: -5px; left: 2px;}
.cl2 {position: relative; top: -5px; left: 2px;}
.cl3 {position: absolute; top: 25px; left: 2px;}
.cl4 {position: fixed; top: 0px;  left: 200px;}
.contain {position: relative; background: yellow; height: 50px;}
</pre>
<hr>
<p>
The following paragraph will contain four positioned images.  Each image is prefaced by a class marker, and each image is numbered so that it is possible to determine which images have been positioned in which places.  The containing 'p' element has a class of 'contain'.   The following is what should happen with each image:
</p>
<ul>
<li>The image should not be offset, as static-position elements ignore the offset properties.  It should scroll with the document.</li>
<li>The image should be offset 5 pixels upward, and 2 pixels to the right.  It should scroll with the document.</li>
<li>The image should be placed 25 pixels below the top edge of the containing block, and 2 pixels to the right of the left edge of the containing block.  It should scroll with the document.</li>
<li>The image should be placed at the top edge of the viewport, and 200 pixels to the right of the left edge of the viewport.  It should <strong>not</strong> scroll with the document.</li>
</ul>
<p class="contain">
[cl1] <img src="pix/num1.gif" class="cl1" alt="image" title="[cl1]"> 
[cl2] <img src="pix/num2.gif" class="cl2" alt="image" title="[cl2]"> 
[cl3] <img src="pix/num3.gif" class="cl3" alt="image" title="[cl3]"> 
[cl4] <img src="pix/num4.gif" class="cl4" alt="image" title="[cl4]"> 
</p>

<p>
An excerpt from section 9.3.1:
</p>

<p>The <a href="visuren.html#propdef-position" class="noxref"><span class="propinst-position">'position'</span></a> and <a href="visuren.html#propdef-float" class="noxref"><span
class="propinst-float">'float'</span></a> properties determine which 
of the CSS2 positioning algorithms is used to calculate 
the position of a box.

<div class="propdef">
<dl><dt>
<span class="index-def" title="'position'"><a name="propdef-position" class="propdef-title"><strong>'position'</strong></a></span>
<dd>
<table class="propinfo" cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0>
<tr valign=baseline><td><em>Value:</em>&nbsp;&nbsp;<td>static | relative | absolute | fixed | <a href="cascade.html#value-def-inherit" class="noxref"><span class="value-inst-inherit">inherit</span></a>

<tr valign=baseline><td><em>Initial:</em>&nbsp;&nbsp;<td>static
<tr valign=baseline><td><em>Applies to:</em>&nbsp;&nbsp;<td>all elements, but not to generated content
<tr valign=baseline><td><em>Inherited:</em>&nbsp;&nbsp;<td>no
<tr valign=baseline><td><em>Percentages:</em>&nbsp;&nbsp;<td>N/A
<tr valign=baseline><td><em>Media:</em>&nbsp;&nbsp;<td><a href="media.html#visual-media-group" class="noxref">visual</a>
</table>
</dl>
</div>


<p>The values of this property have the following meanings:</p>

<dl>
<dt><strong>static</strong>

<dd>The box is a normal box, laid out according to the <a
href="#normal-flow">normal flow</a>. The <a href="visuren.html#propdef-left" class="noxref"><span
class="propinst-left">'left'</span></a> and <a href="visuren.html#propdef-top" class="noxref"><span
class="propinst-top">'top'</span></a> properties do not apply. 

<dt><strong>relative</strong>

<dd>The box's position is calculated according to the <a
href="#normal-flow">normal flow</a> (this is called the position in
normal flow). Then the box is offset <a
href="#relative-positioning">relative</a> to its normal position. When
a box B is relatively positioned, the position of the following box is
calculated as though B were not offset.

<dt><strong>absolute</strong>
<dd> The box's position (and possibly size) is specified
with the <a href="visuren.html#propdef-left" class="noxref"><span class="propinst-left">'left'</span></a>,
<a href="visuren.html#propdef-right" class="noxref"><span class="propinst-right">'right'</span></a>, 
<a href="visuren.html#propdef-top" class="noxref"><span class="propinst-top">'top'</span></a>,
and <a href="visuren.html#propdef-bottom" class="noxref"><span class="propinst-bottom">'bottom'</span></a> properties.
These properties specify offsets with respect to the box's

<a href="#containing-block">containing block</a>. Absolutely
positioned boxes are taken out of the normal flow. This means
they have no impact on the layout of later siblings. Also,
though <a href="#absolutely-positioned">absolutely positioned</a> boxes have margins, they
do not <a href="box.html#collapsing-margins">collapse</a>
with any other margins.

<dt><strong>fixed</strong>
<dd> The box's position is calculated according to the 'absolute'
model, but in addition, the box is <a
href="#fixed-positioning">fixed</a> with respect to some reference. In
the case of <a href="media.html#continuous-media-group">continuous
media</a>, the box is fixed with respect to the <a
href="#viewport">viewport</a> (and doesn't move when scrolled).  In
the case of <a href="media.html#paged-media-group">paged media</a>,
the box is fixed with respect to the page, even if that page is seen
through a <a href="#viewport">viewport</a> (in the case of a
print-preview, for example).</dd>
</dl>
<hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec09-02-05.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec09-03-02a.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/visuren.html#propdef-position">Specification</A>]
<HR>
</body>
</html>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 9.5.1 float</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec09-03-02d.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec09-05-02.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/visuren.html#propdef-float">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>IMG {float: right;}
IMG.cl1 {float: left;}
IMG.cl2 {float: right;}
IMG.cl3 {float: none;}
P.cl4 {float: left; width: 10em; background: yellow;}
SPAN.cl5 {float: right; width: 7em; background: yellow;}
</pre>
<hr>
<P>
<IMG SRC="pix/num1.gif" class="cl1">
[cl1] The image which occurs at the beginning of this paragraph should be floated to the left, and the text is the paragraph should "wrap around" the image.  This is the kind of behavior we've come to expect from Web browsers over the years.
</P>
<P>
<IMG SRC="pix/num2.gif" class="cl2">
[cl2] The image which occurs at the beginning of this paragraph should be floated to the right, and the text is the paragraph should "wrap around" the image.  This is the kind of behavior we've come to expect from Web browsers over the years.
</P>
<P>
<IMG SRC="pix/num3.gif" class="cl3">
[cl3] The image which occurs at the beginning of this paragraph should not be floated at all, and therefore the text is the paragraph should not "wrap around" the image.  Instead, the image should appear as an inline element at the beginning of the paragraph.  This is the kind of behavior we came to expect from Web browsers in the early years.
</P>

<P class="cl4">[cl4] This paragraph has been floated to the left, and has a width of ten (10) em with a yellow background.</P>
<P>
This is an ordinary, unstyled paragraph.  It should "wrap around" the previous paragraph, the one with a class of 'cl4', due to the floatation of the previous paragraph.  In other words, the behavior should be exactly the same as one would expect from the test cases above, or indeed from any surfing done on the Web.
</P>
<BR clear="all">
<P>
This paragraph contains an inline element <SPAN class="cl5">[cl5] with a class of 'cl5'</SPAN> which should float to the right, be seven (7) em wide, and have a yellow background.
</P><hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec09-03-02d.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec09-05-02.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/visuren.html#propdef-float">Specification</A>]

<title>9.8.2 Relative Positioning</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
P.start {line-height: 24px; font-size: 12px; width: 400px;
     color: black; background: white;}
#outer {color: purple; border: 1px solid purple; position: relative; top: -12px;}
#inner {color: blue; border: 1px solid blue; position: relative; top: 12px;}

DIV {background: yellow; height: 50px; width: 250px; margin: 10px;}
IMG.cl1 {position: relative; top: 30%;}
IMG.cl2 {position: relative; right: -30%;}
IMG.cl3 {position: relative; bottom: 30%;}
IMG.cl4 {position: relative; left: 30%;}
IMG.cl5 {position: relative; top: -20px;}
IMG.cl6 {position: relative; right: -20px;}
IMG.cl7 {position: relative; bottom: -20px;}
IMG.cl8 {position: relative; left: -20px;}

SPAN.cl9 {position: relative; top: -1em; left: -5em; color: purple;}
SPAN.cl10 {position: relative; bottom: -1em; right: -5em; color: purple;}</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 9.8.2 Relative Positioning</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec09-05-02.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec09-08-03.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/visuren.html#q27">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>P.start {line-height: 24px; font-size: 12px; width: 400px;
     color: black; background: white;}
#outer {color: purple; border: 1px solid purple; position: relative; top: -12px;}
#inner {color: blue; border: 1px solid blue; position: relative; top: 12px;}

DIV {background: yellow; height: 50px; width: 250px; margin: 10px;}
IMG.cl1 {position: relative; top: 30%;}
IMG.cl2 {position: relative; right: -30%;}
IMG.cl3 {position: relative; bottom: 30%;}
IMG.cl4 {position: relative; left: 30%;}
IMG.cl5 {position: relative; top: -20px;}
IMG.cl6 {position: relative; right: -20px;}
IMG.cl7 {position: relative; bottom: -20px;}
IMG.cl8 {position: relative; left: -20px;}

SPAN.cl9 {position: relative; top: -1em; left: -5em; color: purple;}
SPAN.cl10 {position: relative; bottom: -1em; right: -5em; color: purple;}
</pre>
<hr>
<P class="start">
[start] The beginning of the paragraph contents.
<SPAN ID="outer">[outer] The beginning of the outer SPAN.
<SPAN ID="inner">[inner] The contents of the inner SPAN.</SPAN>
[outer] The end of the outer SPAN.</SPAN>
The end of the paragraph contents.
</P>

<HR>

<P>
The following DIVs have been engineered to create a context for positioning.  The class of each test is noted at the beginning of the DIV.  The percentage offsets should be calculated with respect to the width (250px) or height (50px) of the containing block, depending on the property being tested.
</P>

</DIV>

<head>
<title>9.8.3 Floating a Box</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
P.start {line-height: 24px; font-size: 12px; width: 400px;
     color: black; background: white;}
#outer1 {color: purple; border: 1px solid purple;}
#inner1 {color: blue; border: 1px solid blue; float: right; width: 130px;}
#outer2 {color: purple; border: 1px solid purple;}
#inner2 {color: blue; border: 1px solid blue; float: right; width: 130px;}
#sibling2 {color: maroon; border: 1px solid maroon;}
#outer3 {color: purple; border: 1px solid purple;}
#inner3 {color: blue; border: 1px solid blue; float: right; width: 130px;}
#sibling3 {color: maroon; border: 1px solid maroon; clear: right;}
</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 9.8.3 Floating a Box</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec09-08-02.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec09-08-04.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/visuren.html#propdef-float">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>P.start {line-height: 24px; font-size: 12px; width: 400px;
     color: black; background: white;}
#outer1 {color: purple; border: 1px solid purple;}
#inner1 {color: blue; border: 1px solid blue; float: right; width: 130px;}
#outer2 {color: purple; border: 1px solid purple;}
#inner2 {color: blue; border: 1px solid blue; float: right; width: 130px;}
#sibling2 {color: maroon; border: 1px solid maroon;}
#outer3 {color: purple; border: 1px solid purple;}
#inner3 {color: blue; border: 1px solid blue; float: right; width: 130px;}
#sibling3 {color: maroon; border: 1px solid maroon; clear: right;}

</pre>
<hr>
<P class="start">
[start] The beginning of the paragraph contents.
<SPAN ID="outer1">[outer1] The beginning of the outer SPAN.
<SPAN ID="inner1">[inner1] The contents of the inner SPAN.</SPAN>
[outer] The end of the outer SPAN.</SPAN>
The end of the paragraph contents.
</P>

<P class="start">
[start] The beginning of the paragraph contents.
<SPAN ID="outer2">[outer2] The beginning of the outer SPAN.
<SPAN ID="inner2">[inner2] The contents of the inner SPAN.</SPAN>
<SPAN ID="sibling2">[sibling2] The sibling's contents.</SPAN>
[outer] The end of the outer SPAN.</SPAN>
The end of the paragraph contents.
</P>

<P class="start">
[start] The beginning of the paragraph contents.
<SPAN ID="outer3">[outer3] The beginning of the outer SPAN.
<SPAN ID="inner3">[inner3] The contents of the inner SPAN.</SPAN>
<SPAN ID="sibling3">[sibling3] The sibling's contents.</SPAN>
[outer] The end of the outer SPAN.</SPAN>
The end of the paragraph contents.
</P>

##### sec09-08-04.htm #####
<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/html4/loose.dtd"> 
<html>
<head>
<title>9.8.4 Absolute Positioning</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
P.start {line-height: 24px; font-size: 12px; width: 400px;
     color: black; background: white; position: relative;}
#outer1 {color: purple; border: 1px solid purple; position: absolute; top: 100px; left: 100px; width: 200px;}
#inner1 {color: blue; border: 1px solid blue;}
#outer2 {color: purple; border: 1px solid purple; position: relative;}
#inner2 {color: blue; border: 1px solid blue; position: absolute; top: 100px; left: -100px; width: 200px;}

P.barnote {position: relative; margin-right: 2em; left: 2em; width: 50%;}
SPAN.mark {position: absolute; top: auto; left: -2em; color: maroon;}

DIV {position: relative; background: yellow; height: 50px; width: 250px; margin: 10px;}
IMG.cl1 {position: absolute; top: 30%;}
IMG.cl2 {position: absolute; right: 30%;}
IMG.cl3 {position: absolute; bottom: 30%;}
IMG.cl4 {position: absolute; left: 30%;}
IMG.cl5 {position: absolute; top: 0; left: 0;}
IMG.cl6 {position: absolute; top: 0; right: 100%;}
IMG.cl7 {position: absolute; bottom: 100%; left: 0;}
IMG.cl8 {position: absolute; bottom: 100%; right: 100%;}
</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 9.8.4 Absolute Positioning</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec09-08-03.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec09-09-01.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/visuren.html#q29">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>P.start {line-height: 24px; font-size: 12px; width: 400px;
     color: black; background: white; position: relative;}
#outer1 {color: purple; border: 1px solid purple; position: absolute; top: 100px; left: 100px; width: 200px;}
#inner1 {color: blue; border: 1px solid blue;}
#outer2 {color: purple; border: 1px solid purple; position: relative;}
#inner2 {color: blue; border: 1px solid blue; position: absolute; top: 100px; left: -100px; width: 200px;}

P.barnote {position: relative; margin-right: 2em; left: 2em; width: 50%;}
SPAN.mark {position: absolute; top: auto; left: -2em; color: maroon;}

DIV {position: relative; background: yellow; height: 50px; width: 250px; margin: 10px;}
IMG.cl1 {position: absolute; top: 30%;}
IMG.cl2 {position: absolute; right: 30%;}
IMG.cl3 {position: absolute; bottom: 30%;}
IMG.cl4 {position: absolute; left: 30%;}
IMG.cl5 {position: absolute; top: 0; left: 0;}
IMG.cl6 {position: absolute; top: 0; right: 100%;}
IMG.cl7 {position: absolute; bottom: 100%; left: 0;}
IMG.cl8 {position: absolute; bottom: 100%; right: 100%;}

</pre>
<hr>
<P class="start">
[start] The beginning of the paragraph contents.
<SPAN ID="outer1">[outer1] The beginning of the outer SPAN.
<SPAN ID="inner1">[inner1] The contents of the inner SPAN.</SPAN>
[outer] The end of the outer SPAN.</SPAN>
The end of the paragraph contents.
</P>

<P class="start">
[start] The beginning of the paragraph contents.
<SPAN ID="outer2">[outer2] The beginning of the outer SPAN.
<SPAN ID="inner2">[inner2] The contents of the inner SPAN.</SPAN>
[outer] The end of the outer SPAN.</SPAN>
The end of the paragraph contents.
</P>

<HR>

<P class="barnote">
[barnote] This paragraph contains an SPAN element (with a class of 'mark') which will cause the SPANned text to be "floated" to the beginning of the line in which it occurs.  In other words, a pair of red dashes will appear at the beginning of the line containing THIS <SPAN class="mark">--</SPAN> word.
</P>

<HR>

<P>
The following DIVs have been engineered to create a context for positioning.  The class of each test is noted at the beginning of the DIV.  The percentage offsets should be calculated with respect to the width (250px) or height (50px) of the containing block, depending on the property being tested.
</P>
<DIV>
[cl1] <IMG SRC="pix/num1.gif" class="cl1">
</DIV>
<DIV>
[cl2] <IMG SRC="pix/num2.gif" class="cl2">
</DIV>
<DIV>
[cl3] <IMG SRC="pix/num3.gif" class="cl3">
</DIV>
<DIV>
[cl4] <IMG SRC="pix/num4.gif" class="cl4">
</DIV>
<HR>
<P>
The following four images have been absolutely positioned without a containing element, and so are positioned with respect to the BODY element, which is their parent element.  The images should be scrolled with the document, should any scrolling occur.
</P>
[cl5] <IMG SRC="pix/num5.gif" class="cl5">
[cl6] <IMG SRC="pix/num6.gif" class="cl6">
[cl7] <IMG SRC="pix/num7.gif" class="cl7">
[cl8] <IMG SRC="pix/num8.gif" class="cl8">
