<style type="text/css">
.test {background: lime;}
.cl1 {background: green;}
.cl2 {background: green url(pix/smgr-bg.gif) top center repeat-x;}
.cl3 {background: silver url(pix/crosshair.gif) center no-repeat;}
.cl4 {background: url(pix/crosshair.gif) no-repeat;}
.cl5 {background: transparent url(pix/vertical-wave.gif) center repeat-y fixed;}
.parent {background: silver url(pix/crosshair2.gif) top right repeat-x;}
.inh {background: #FCC url(pix/redsqr.gif) repeat-y;}
</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 14.2.1 background </h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec14-02-01e.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec15-02-02.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/colors.html#propdef-background">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>.test {background: lime;}
.cl1 {background: green;}
.cl2 {background: green url(pix/smgr-bg.gif) top center repeat-x;}
.cl3 {background: silver url(pix/crosshair.gif) center no-repeat;}
.cl4 {background: url(pix/crosshair.gif) no-repeat;}
.cl5 {background: transparent url(pix/vertical-wave.gif) center repeat-y fixed;}
.parent {background: silver url(pix/crosshair2.gif) top right repeat-x;}
.inh {background: #FCC url(pix/redsqr.gif) repeat-y;}

</pre>
<hr>
<p class="test">
[test] This 'p' element should have a lime background.
</p>
<p class="test cl1">
[test cl1] This 'p' element should have a green background.  This is distinct from a lime background.
</p>
<p class="test cl2">
test cl2] This 'p' element should have a green background, except along the top, where a green-grid strip should originate at the top center of the background area and repeat to both the right and the left of that point.
</p>
<p class="test cl3">
test cl3] This 'p' element should have a silver background and a single crosshair image at the center of the background area.  This image should not tile in any direction.
</p>
<p class="test cl4">
test cl4] This 'p' element should have a single crosshair image at the top left corner of its background area, and the rest of the background should be transparent.  If the rest of the background is lime, then the test has been failed.
</p>
<p class="test cl5">
test cl5] This 'p' element should have a wavy stripe down the center of its background area, and this stripe should remain stationary while the document is scrolled.  In other words, the element should seem as if it is a moving window through which different parts of the wavy image are visible.  In order to make the effect more obvious, extra text is appended to the content of this element in order to increase its height.  Also consider resizing the browser window to be more narrow so that the element becomes taller and is (visually) pushed further down in the document.
</p>
<p>
A relevant quotation from the CSS2 specification:
</p>
<div class="propdef">
<dl><dt>
<span class="index-def" title="'background'"><a name="propdef-background" class="propdef-title"><strong>'background'</strong></a></span>
<dd>
<table class="propinfo" cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0>

<tr valign=baseline><td><em>Value:</em>&nbsp;&nbsp;<td>[<a href="colors.html#propdef-background-color" class="noxref"><span class="propinst-background-color">&lt;'background-color'&gt;</span></a> || <a href="colors.html#propdef-background-image" class="noxref"><span class="propinst-background-image">&lt;'background-image'&gt;</span></a> || <a href="colors.html#propdef-background-repeat" class="noxref"><span class="propinst-background-repeat">&lt;'background-repeat'&gt;</span></a>
|| <a href="colors.html#propdef-background-attachment" class="noxref"><span class="propinst-background-attachment">&lt;'background-attachment'&gt;</span></a> || <a href="colors.html#propdef-background-position" class="noxref"><span class="propinst-background-position">&lt;'background-position'&gt;</span></a>] | <a href="cascade.html#value-def-inherit" class="noxref"><span class="value-inst-inherit">inherit</span></a>

<tr valign=baseline><td><em>Initial:</em>&nbsp;&nbsp;<td>not defined for shorthand properties
<tr valign=baseline><td><em>Applies to:</em>&nbsp;&nbsp;<td>all elements
<tr valign=baseline><td><em>Inherited:</em>&nbsp;&nbsp;<td>no
<tr valign=baseline><td><em>Percentages:</em>&nbsp;&nbsp;<td>allowed on 'background-position'
<tr valign=baseline><td><em>Media:</em>&nbsp;&nbsp;<td><a href="media.html#visual-media-group" class="noxref">visual</a>
</table>
</dl>
</div>

<p> The <a href="colors.html#propdef-background" class="noxref"><span class="propinst-background">'background'</span></a> property
is a shorthand property for setting the individual background
properties (i.e., <a href="colors.html#propdef-background-color" class="noxref"><span
class="propinst-background-color">'background-color'</span></a>, <a href="colors.html#propdef-background-image" class="noxref"><span
class="propinst-background-image">'background-image'</span></a>, <a href="colors.html#propdef-background-repeat" class="noxref"><span
class="propinst-background-repeat">'background-repeat'</span></a>, <a href="colors.html#propdef-background-attachment" class="noxref"><span
class="propinst-background-attachment">'background-attachment'</span></a>
and <a href="colors.html#propdef-background-position" class="noxref"><span
class="propinst-background-position">'background-position'</span></a>) at
the same place in the style sheet.
</p>

<p> The <a href="colors.html#propdef-background" class="noxref"><span class="propinst-background">'background'</span></a> property
first sets all the individual background properties to their initial
values, then assigns explicit values given in the declaration.
</p>
<hr><div class="parent">
[parent] This 'div' element is the parent of another 'div' that is used to test inheritance.  The parent has a silver background and a horizontal stripe of green crosshair images running along the top side of its background area, beginning in the top right corner of the background area.
<div class="inh1" style="background: inherit;">
[inh1] This 'div' element should have a silver background and a horizontal stripe of green crosshair images running along the top side of its background area, beginning in the top right corner of the background area, the same as its parent, as it has a style attribute set to inherit the <code>background</code> value.  If the background is light red with a bright red vertical stripe through its center, the test has been failed.
</div>
This is the end of the parent element.
</div><hr>

</P>
<P>
<B>[B] The font for this bold element should be normal (boldface made lighter).</B>
</P>
<P class="cl3">
[cl3] The font for this paragraph should be bolder than normal.
</P>
<H4>This is a heading-4.</H4>
<H4 class="cl3">[cl3] This is a bolder heading-4.</H4>

<UL>
<LI class="cl5w1">[cl5w1] The font for this list item should be weight 100.</LI>
<LI class="cl5w2">[cl5w2] The font for this list item should be weight 200.</LI>
<LI class="cl5w3">[cl5w3] The font for this list item should be weight 300.</LI>
<LI class="cl5w4">[cl5w4] The font for this list item should be weight 400.</LI>
<LI class="cl5w5">[cl5w5] The font for this list item should be weight 500.</LI>
<LI class="cl5w6">[cl5w6] The font for this list item should be weight 600.</LI>
<LI class="cl5w7">[cl5w7] The font for this list item should be weight 700.</LI>
<LI class="cl5w8">[cl5w8] The font for this list item should be weight 800.</LI>
<LI class="cl5w9">[cl5w9] The font for this list item should be weight 900.</LI>
</UL>

<P>
The following list should contain list items in which the content of each item is the same weight.
</P>
<UL>
<LI><SPAN class="cl4">[cl4] normal</SPAN>, <SPAN class="cl5w4">[cl5w4] 400</SPAN>
<LI><SPAN class="cl1">[cl1] bold</SPAN>, <SPAN class="cl5w7">[cl5w7] 700</SPAN>
</UL>
<hr><div class="parent">
[div.parent] This DIV has been set with parental styles.  The inline elements within this DIV are enclosed in square brackets in order to more easily discern their placement.
<div class="inh1" style="font-weight: inherit;">
[div.inh1] This DIV should use a normally weighted font for its display, as it has a style attribute set to inherit the <code>font-weight</code> value. [/div.inh1]
</div>
<div class="inh2" style="font-weight: inherit;">
[div.inh2] This DIV should use a normally weighted font for its display, as it has a style attribute set to inherit the <code>font-weight</code> value. [/div.inh2]
</div>
This is the end of the parent DIV. [/div.parent]
</div><hr>

[cl3] The font of this paragraph should be smaller than unstyled text.
</P>

</P>
<P class="cl15">
[cl15] The font of this paragraph should be two em tall.
</P>
<P class="cl16">
[cl16] The font of this paragraph should be three ex tall.

</p>

</p>
<p class="cl-sys-d">

</p>

</p>
<p class="cl-sys-f">

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 16.1 text-indent</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec15-02-05.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec16-02.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/text.html#propdef-text-indent">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>.cl1 {text-indent: 0.5in; background: aqua;}
.cl2 {text-indent: 2cm; background: aqua;}
.cl3 {text-indent: 20mm; background: aqua;}
.cl4 {text-indent: 24pt; background: aqua;}
.cl5 {text-indent: 2pc; background: aqua;}
.cl6 {text-indent: 2em; background: aqua;}
.cl7 {text-indent: 2ex; background: aqua;}
.cl8 {text-indent: 50%; background: aqua;}
.cl9 {text-indent: 25px; background: aqua;}
blockquote {text-indent: 50%; background: aqua;}
div.parent {text-indent: 50%; width: 400px;}
div.inh1 {text-indent: 10px; margin: 25px;}
div.inh2 {text-indent: 10%; margin: 25px;}

</pre>
<hr>
<P class="cl1">
[cl1] The first line of this paragraph should be indented half an inch.  No other line in the paragraph should be so indented, although line-wrapping will have to occur in order to properly test this assertion.
</P>
<P class="cl2">
[cl2] The first line of this sentence should be indented two centimeters.  No other line in the paragraph should be so indented, although line-wrapping will have to occur in order to properly test this assertion.
</P>
<P class="cl3">
[cl3] The first line of this sentence should be indented twenty millimeters.  No other line in the paragraph should be so indented, although line-wrapping will have to occur in order to properly test this assertion.
</P>
<P class="cl4">
[cl4] The first line of this sentence should be indented twenty-four points.  No other line in the paragraph should be so indented, although line-wrapping will have to occur in order to properly test this assertion.
</P>
<P class="cl5">
[cl5] The first line of this sentence should be indented two picas.  No other line in the paragraph should be so indented, although line-wrapping will have to occur in order to properly test this assertion.
</P>
<P class="cl6">
[cl6] The first line of this sentence should be indented two em.  No other line in the paragraph should be so indented, although line-wrapping will have to occur in order to properly test this assertion.
</P>
<P class="cl7">
[cl7] The first line of this sentence should be indented two ex.  No other line in the paragraph should be so indented, although line-wrapping will have to occur in order to properly test this assertion.
</P>
<P class="cl8">
[cl8] The first line of this sentence should be indented halfway across the page, but the rest of it should be flush with the normal left margin of the page.  Line-wrapping will have to occur in order to properly test this assertion.
</P>
<P class="cl9">
[cl9] The first line of this sentence should be indented 25 pixels, but the rest of it should be flush with the normal left margin of the page.  Line-wrapping will have to occur in order to properly test this assertion.
</P>
<P class="cl1">
[cl1] Only the first line of this sentence should be indented half an inch,<BR>
no matter where the lines might start, and<BR>
<EM>regardless of any other markup</EM> which may be present.
</P>
<blockquote>
[blockquote] The first line of this BLOCKQUOTE element should have a text indent equal to 50% of the BODY element's width, since BLOCKQUOTE is a child of BODY.  No other line in the element should be so indented, although line-wrapping will have to occur in order to properly test this assertion.
</blockquote>
<hr><div class="parent">
[div.parent] This DIV has been set with parental styles.  The inline elements within this DIV are enclosed in square brackets in order to more easily discern their placement.
<div class="inh1" style="text-indent: inherit;">
[div.inh1] This DIV should have its first line indented by half the width of its parent element, as it has a style attribute set to inherit the <code>text-indent</code> value. [/div.inh1]
</div>
<div class="inh2" style="text-indent: inherit;">
[div.inh2] This DIV should have its first line indented by half the width of its parent element, as it has a style attribute set to inherit the <code>text-indent</code> value. [/div.inh2]
</div>
This is the end of the parent DIV. [/div.parent]
</div><hr>

[cl3] The text of this paragraph should be stricken (linethrough).
</P>
<P class="cl4">
[cl4] The text of this paragraph should be blinking.  (It is not required, however, that UAs support this behavior.)
</P>

<P class="cl1">
[cl1] The text of this paragraph should be underlined.  The boldfaced text in this paragraph <B class="cl5">[cl5] should also be underlined</B>.  This is because the parent's underline will 'span' the boldfaced text, even if the inline element has no underline of its own.
</P>

<P class="cl6">
[cl6] The text of this paragraph should be underlined and overlined.
</P>
<P class="cl7">
[cl7] The text of this paragraph should be underlined, overlined, and stricken.
</P>
<P class="cl7">
</P>
<P>
There should be nothing visible between this paragraph and the one above (there is an empty paragraph element with class of seven between them).
</P>
<P class="cl1">
[cl1] Text decorations only apply to the text of an element, so the image at the end of this sentence should <EM>not</EM> be overlined: <IMG SRC="pix/oransqr.gif" class="two" alt="[Image]">.  The underline of the parent element should hold true beneath the image, however, since text-decoration 'spans' child elements.
</P>
<P style="color: green;" class="cl1">
[cl1] The underlining <SPAN style="color: blue;">in this paragraph</SPAN> should be green, no matter what the <SPAN style="color: black;">text color may be</SPAN>.
</P>
<P class="cl1">
[cl1] The colors of the <SPAN style="color: purple;">underlining</SPAN> in <SPAN style="color: blue;">this paragraph</SPAN> should be <SPAN style="color: gray;">the same as that of the parent text</SPAN> (that is, the first word in the sentence, which should be black).
</P>

[div.inh2] This DIV should use no text decoration for its display, as it has a style attribute set to inherit the <code>text-decoration</code> value. [/div.inh2]
</div>
This is the end of the parent DIV. [/div.parent]

<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/html4/loose.dtd"> 
<html>
<head>
<title>16.5 text-transform</title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
.ttn {text-transform: none;}
.cap {text-transform: capitalize;}
.upp {text-transform: uppercase;}
.low {text-transform: lowercase;}
div.parent {text-transform: none;}
div.inh1 {text-transform: uppercase;}
div.inh2 {text-transform: lowercase;}
</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 16.5 text-transform</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec16-04b.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec16-06.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/text.html#propdef-text-transform">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>.ttn {text-transform: none;}
.cap {text-transform: capitalize;}
.upp {text-transform: uppercase;}
.low {text-transform: lowercase;}
div.parent {text-transform: none;}
div.inh1 {text-transform: uppercase;}
div.inh2 {text-transform: lowercase;}

</pre>
<hr>
<P CLASS="ttn">[ttn] This page tests the 'text-transform' property of CSS1.  This paragraph has no text transformation and should appear normal.
</P>
<P CLASS="cap">[cap] This paragraph is capitalized and the first letter in each word should therefore appear in uppercase. Words that are in uppercase in the source (e.g. USA) should remain so. There should be a capital letter after a non-breaking&nbsp;space (&amp;nbsp;). Both those characters appear in the previous sentence.
</P>
<P>Words with inline elements inside them should only capitalize the first letter of the word. Therefore, the last word in this sentence should have one, and only one, capital <SPAN CLASS="cap">[cap] le<SPAN>tt</SPAN>er</SPAN>. 
</P>
<P CLASS="upp">[upp] This paragraph is uppercased and small characters in the source (e.g. a and &aring;) should therefore appear in uppercase.  In the last sentence, however, <SPAN class="ttn">[ttn] the last eight words should not be uppercase</SPAN>.
</P>
<P CLASS="low">[low] This paragraph is lowercased and capital characters in the source (e.g. A and &Aring;) should therefore appear in lowercase.
</P>
<hr><div class="parent">
[div.parent] This DIV has been set with parental styles.  The inline elements within this DIV are enclosed in square brackets in order to more easily discern their placement.
<div class="inh1" style="text-transform: inherit;">
[div.inh1] This DIV should use no text transformation in for its display, as it has a style attribute set to inherit the <code>text-transform</code> value. [/div.inh1]
</div>
<div class="inh2" style="text-transform: inherit;">
[div.inh2] This DIV should use no text transformation in for its display, as it has a style attribute set to inherit the <code>text-transform</code> value. [/div.inh2]
</div>
This is the end of the parent DIV. [/div.parent]
</div><hr>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec16-04b.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec16-06.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/text.html#propdef-text-transform">Specification</A>]
<HR>
</body>
</html>

.cl1 {white-space: pre;}
.cl2 {white-space: nowrap;}
.cl3 {white-space: normal;}
div.parent {white-space: normal;}
div.inh1 {white-space: pre;}
div.inh2 {white-space: nowrap;}
</style>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 16.6 white-space</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec16-05.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec17-04-01.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/text.html#propdef-white-space">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>.cl1 {white-space: pre;}
.cl2 {white-space: nowrap;}
.cl3 {white-space: normal;}
div.parent {white-space: normal;}
div.inh1 {white-space: pre;}
div.inh2 {white-space: nowrap;}

</pre>
<hr>
<P class="cl1">
[cl1] This paragraph should     show extra space  where there    would ordinarily         not be any.
     There should also be preservation of returns
as this sentence
     very clearly demonstrates.
</P>

<P class="cl2">
[cl2] This paragraph should not word-wrap, no matter how long the paragraph might be or over how many lines it would ordinarily wrap, as it has been set to <CODE>white-space: nowrap</CODE> and that should have the obvious effect.
</P>

<P class="cl1">
[cl1] This paragraph      should     show extra   space, <SPAN class="cl3">[cl3] except in the       second half</SPAN>.
</P>
<hr><div class="parent">
[div.parent] This DIV has been set with parental styles.  The inline elements within this DIV are enclosed in square brackets in order to more easily discern their placement.
<div class="inh1" style="white-space: inherit;">
[div.inh1] This DIV should use normal white space handling for its display, as it has a style attribute set to inherit the <code>white-space</code> value. [/div.inh1]
</div>
<div class="inh2" style="white-space: inherit;">
[div.inh2] This DIV should use normal white space handling for its display, as it has a style attribute set to inherit the <code>white-space</code> value. [/div.inh2]
</div>
This is the end of the parent DIV. [/div.parent]
</div><hr>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 17.5.2 table-layout </h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec17-04-01.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec17-06.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/tables.html#propdef-table-layout">Specification</A>]

<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>table {background: gray; width: 300px;}
table td {background: #FF9; color: black;}
.r1c2 {width: 100px;}
.r2c1 {width: 150px;}
.r3c3 {width: 100px;}
.cl1 {table-layout: fixed;}
.cl2 {table-layout: auto;}

</pre>
<hr>
<p>
In the following table, the cells should extend outside of the 'table' element itself, because their aggregate widths are greater than 300px.  The table should <strong>not</strong> expand to contain the cells.
</p>
<table class="cl1">
<tr>
<td>[cl1]</td><td class="r1c2">r1c2</td><td>r1c3</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="r2c1">r2c1</td><td>r2c2</td><td>r2c3</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>r3c1</td><td>r3c2</td><td class="r3c3">r3c3</td>
</tr>
</table>

<p>
In the following table, the cells should <strong>not</strong> extend outside of the 'table' element itself, even though their aggregate widths are greater than 300px.  The table should instead expand to contain the cells.
</p>
<table class="cl2">
<tr>
<td>[cl2]</td><td class="r1c2">r1c2</td><td>r1c3</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="r2c1">r2c1</td><td>r2c2</td><td>r2c3</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>r3c1</td><td>r3c2</td><td class="r3c3">r3c3</td>
</tr>
</table>

<head>
<title>17.6 border-collapse </title>
<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">
<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="screen" href="base.css">
<style type="text/css">
table {background: gray; width: 300px; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 3px;}
table td {background: #FF9; color: black; border: 2px outset silver;}
.cl1 {border-collapse: separate;}
.cl2 {border-collapse: collapse;}

table.cl3 { border-collapse: collapse; border: 5px solid yellow; }
table.cl3 col#col1 { border: 3px solid black; }
table.cl3 td { border: 1px solid red; padding: 1em; }
table.cl3 td.solid-blue { border: 5px dashed blue; }
table.cl3 td.solid-green { border: 5px solid green; }

</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 17.6 border-collapse </h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec17-05-02.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec17-06-01a.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/tables.html#propdef-border-collapse">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>table {background: gray; width: 300px; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 3px;}
table td {background: #FF9; color: black; border: 2px outset silver;}
.cl1 {border-collapse: separate;}
.cl2 {border-collapse: collapse;}

table.cl3 { border-collapse: collapse; border: 5px solid yellow; }
table.cl3 col#col1 { border: 3px solid black; }
table.cl3 td { border: 1px solid red; padding: 1em; }
table.cl3 td.solid-blue { border: 5px dashed blue; }
table.cl3 td.solid-green { border: 5px solid green; }


</pre>
<hr>
<p>
The following 'table' element should have 3 pixels of space between its cells (both horizontally and vertically) and 10 pixels of padding around the outer edge of the table.  In addition, each cell should have a two-pixel outset border, with each border separate from the others.
</p>
<table class="cl1">
<tr>
<td>[cl1]</td><td class="r1c2">r1c2</td><td>r1c3</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="r2c1">r2c1</td><td>r2c2</td><td>r2c3</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>r3c1</td><td>r3c2</td><td class="r3c3">r3c3</td>
</tr>
</table>

<p>
The following 'table' element should <strong>not</strong> have 3 pixels of space between its cells (both horizontally and vertically), not should it have 10 pixels of padding around the outer edge of the table.  The cells should not be separated except by their borders, and the borders should appear to "merge" so that cells share borders.
</p>
<table class="cl2">
<tr>
<td>[cl2]</td><td class="r1c2">r1c2</td><td>r1c3</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="r2c1">r2c1</td><td>r2c2</td><td>r2c3</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>r3c1</td><td>r3c2</td><td class="r3c3">r3c3</td>
</tr>
</table>

<p>
The following 'table' element, with a class of 'cl3', is a test of the collapsed-borders model.
</p>
<table class="cl3">
<col id="col1"><col id="col2"><col id="col3">
<tr id="row1">
    <td class="col1"> 1
    <td> 2
    <td> 3
</tr>
<tr id="row2">
    <td class="col1"> 4 
    <td class="solid-blue"> 5
    <td class="solid-green"> 6
</tr>
<tr id="row3">
    <td class="col1"> 7
    <td> 8
    <td> 9
</tr>
<tr id="row4">
    <td class="col1"> 10
    <td> 11
    <td> 12
</tr>
<tr id="row5">
    <td class="col1"> 13
    <td> 14
    <td> 15
</tr>
</table>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 17.6.1 empty-cells </h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec17-06-01a.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec18-01.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/tables.html#propdef-empty-cells">Specification</A>]

<pre>table {background: gray; width: 300px; border-collapse: separate;}

.cl2, .cl3 {empty-cells: hide;}

<p>
The empty cell in the middle of the following 'table' element should be rendered, including its background and borders.

<table class="cl1">
<tr>

</tr>

</tr>
<tr>
<td>r3c1</td><td>r3c2</td><td class="r3c3">r3c3</td>
</tr>
</table>

<p>
The empty cell in the middle of the following 'table' element should <strong>not</strong> be rendered at all.  There should instead be a blank spot in the middle of the 'table'.
</p>
<table class="cl2">
<tr>
<td>[cl2]</td><td class="r1c2">r1c2</td><td>r1c3</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="r2c1">r2c1</td><td></td><td>r2c3</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>r3c1</td><td>r3c2</td><td class="r3c3">r3c3</td>
</tr>
</table>


<p>
The second row in the following 'table' element, which contains only empty cells, should <strong>not</strong> be rendered at all.  The table should be drawn as if the entire row had been set to 'display: none'.
</p>
<table class="cl2">
<tr>
<td>[cl3]</td><td class="r1c2">r1c2</td><td>r1c3</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="r2c1"></td><td></td><td></td>
</tr>

</tr>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 18.1 cursor</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec17-06-01b.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec18-02.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/ui.html#propdef-cursor">Specification</A>]

<pre>TD {background: white;}
.cl1 {cursor: auto;}

.cl5 {cursor: move;}

.cl7 {cursor: e-resize;}
.cl8 {cursor: s-resize;}
.cl9 {cursor: w-resize;}
.cl10 {cursor: ne-resize;}
.cl11 {cursor: se-resize;}
.cl12 {cursor: sw-resize;}
.cl13 {cursor: nw-resize;}

.cl15 {cursor: wait;}
.cl16 {cursor: help;}
.cl17 {cursor: url(Globe.ani);}

div.inh1 {cursor: crosshair;}
div.inh2 {cursor: help;}

</pre>
<hr>
<table border="1" cellspacing="5" cellpadding="5">
<tr> 
<td class="cl1">[cl1] auto</td>
<td class="cl2">[cl2] default</td>
<td class="cl3">[cl3] crosshair</td>
<td class="cl4">[cl4] pointer</td>
<td class="cl5">[cl5] move</td>
</tr>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 18.2 User preferences for colors</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec18-01.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec18-04a.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/ui.html#system-colors">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>.cl1 {color: ActiveBorder;}
.cl2 {color: ActiveCaption;}
.cl3 {color: AppWorkspace;}
.cl4 {color: Background;}
.cl5 {color: ButtonFace;}
.cl6 {color: ButtonHighlight;}
.cl7 {color: ButtonShadow;}
.cl8 {color: ButtonText;}
.cl9 {color: CaptionText;}
.cl10 {color: GrayText;}
.cl11 {color: Highlight;}
.cl12 {color: HighlightText;}
.cl13 {color: InactiveBorder;}
.cl14 {color: InactiveCaption;}
.cl15 {color: InactiveCaptionText;}
.cl16 {color: InfoBackground;}
.cl17 {color: InfoText;}
.cl18 {color: Menu;}
.cl19 {color: MenuText;}
.cl20 {color: Scrollbar;}
.cl21 {color: ThreeDDarkShadow;}
.cl22 {color: ThreeDFace;}
.cl23 {color: ThreeDHighlight;}
.cl24 {color: ThreeDLightShadow;}
.cl25 {color: ThreeDShadow;}
.cl26 {color: Window;}
.cl27 {color: WindowFrame;}
.cl28 {color: WindowText;}

</pre>
<hr>
<P>
The list items in the following list are all set to various colors.  These should match elements of the user agent's operating system or other computing environment.
</P>

<UL>
<LI class="cl1">[cl1] This list item's foreground should match an active window border.
<LI class="cl2">[cl2] This list item's foreground should match an active window caption.
<LI class="cl3">[cl3] This list item's foreground should match an application's (not a document's) background.
<LI class="cl4">[cl4] This list item's foreground should match the desktop background.
<LI class="cl5">[cl5] This list item's foreground should match a button's face.
<LI class="cl6">[cl6] This list item's foreground should match the specular highlight on a button.
<LI class="cl7">[cl7] This list item's foreground should match the shadow on a button.
<LI class="cl8">[cl8] This list item's foreground should match the text of a button.
<LI class="cl9">[cl9] This list item's foreground should match caption text.
<LI class="cl10">[cl10] This list item's foreground should match disabled text.
<LI class="cl11">[cl11] This list item's foreground should match a highlighted control.
<LI class="cl12">[cl12] This list item's foreground should match the text of a highlighted control.
<LI class="cl13">[cl13] This list item's foreground should match an inactive window border.
<LI class="cl14">[cl14] This list item's foreground should match an inactive window caption.
<LI class="cl15">[cl15] This list item's foreground should match the text of an inactive caption.
<LI class="cl16">[cl16] This list item's foreground should match the background color of tooltips.
<LI class="cl17">[cl17] This list item's foreground should match the text of tooltips.
<LI class="cl18">[cl18] This list item's foreground should match a menu's background.
<LI class="cl19">[cl19] This list item's foreground should match the text of a menu.
<LI class="cl20">[cl20] This list item's foreground should match the gray areas of a scrollbar.
<LI class="cl21">[cl21] This list item's foreground should match the dark shadow of any 3D display element.
<LI class="cl22">[cl22] This list item's foreground should match the face of any 3D display element.
<LI class="cl23">[cl23] This list item's foreground should match the highlight of any 3D display element.
<LI class="cl24">[cl24] This list item's foreground should match the the light shadow of any 3D display element.
<LI class="cl25">[cl25] This list item's foreground should match the dark shadow in any 3D display element.
<LI class="cl26">[cl26] This list item's foreground should match the background of a window.
<LI class="cl27">[cl27] This list item's foreground should match the frame of a window.
<LI class="cl28">[cl28] This list item's foreground should match the text in a window.
</UL>
<hr>[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec18-01.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec18-04a.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/ui.html#system-colors">Specification</A>]

<meta http-equiv="Content-Style-Type" content="text/css">

<style type="text/css">
INPUT {border: 3px solid gray;}
.cl1 {outline: 2px dotted green;}
.cl2 {outline: 1em double green;}
.cl3 {outline: thick solid invert;}
div.parent {outline: none;}
div.inh1 {outline: 10px solid red;}
div.inh2 {outline: 1em inset red;}</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 18.4 outline</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec18-02.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec18-04b.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/ui.html#propdef-outline">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>INPUT {border: 3px solid gray;}
.cl1 {outline: 2px dotted green;}
.cl2 {outline: 1em double green;}
.cl3 {outline: thick solid invert;}
div.parent {outline: none;}
div.inh1 {outline: 10px solid red;}
div.inh2 {outline: 1em inset red;}
</pre>
<hr>
<form>
<p>
Here's an input <input type="text" size="10" class="cl1"> whose outline (when in focus) should be 2 pixels wide, dotted, and green.  The outline should be drawn to the outside of the element border.
</p>
<p>
Here's an input <input type="text" size="10" class="cl2"> whose outline (when in focus) should be 1em wide, double, and green.  The outline should be drawn to the outside of the element border.
</p>
<p>
Here's an input <input type="text" size="10" class="cl3"> whose outline (when in focus) should be as wide as "thick", solid, and invert the background.  The outline should be drawn to the outside of the element border.
</p>
</form><hr><div class="parent">
[div.parent] This DIV has been set with parental styles.  The inline elements within this DIV are enclosed in square brackets in order to more easily discern their placement.
<div class="inh1" style="outline: inherit;">
[div.inh1] This DIV should have no outline under any circumstances, as it has a style attribute set to inherit the <code>outline</code> value. [/div.inh1]
</div>
<div class="inh2" style="outline: inherit;">
[div.inh2] This DIV should have no outline under any circumstances, as it has a style attribute set to inherit the <code>outline</code> value. [/div.inh2]
</div>
This is the end of the parent DIV. [/div.parent]
</div><hr>

div.inh2 {outline-width: 1em;}</style>
</head>

<body>
 <h2>CSS2 Test Suite: 18.4 outline-width</h2>
[<A HREF="index.html">index page</A>] [<I>section</I>] [<A HREF="sec18-04a.htm">Previous</A>] [<A HREF="sec18-04c.htm">Next</A>] [<A HREF="http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS2/ui.html#propdef-outline-width">Specification</A>]
<HR>
<p>The style declarations contained within this page:</p>
<pre>INPUT {border: 3px solid gray; outline-style: solid;}
.cl1 {outline-width: 2px;}
.cl2 {outline-width: 1em;}
.cl3 {outline-width: thick;}
div.parent {outline-width: 1px;}
div.inh1 {outline-width: 10px;}
div.inh2 {outline-width: 1em;}
</pre>
<hr>
<p>
Note that the following tests are valid only if the property <code>outline-style</code> is supported.
</p>
<form>
<p>
Here's an input <input type="text" size="10" class="cl1"> whose outline (when in focus) should be 2 pixels wide, solid, and the same color as the element's foreground (black).  The outline should be drawn to the outside of the element border.
</p>
<p>
Here's an input <input type="text" size="10" class="cl2"> whose outline (when in focus) should be 1em wide, solid, and the same color as the element's foreground (black). The outline should be drawn to the outside of the element border.
</p>
<p>
Here's an input <input type="text" size="10" class="cl3"> whose outline (when in focus) should be thick, solid, and the same color as the element's foreground (black).  The outline should be drawn to the outside of the element border.
</p>
</form><hr><div class="parent">
[div.parent] This DIV has been set with parental styles.  The inline elements within this DIV are enclosed in square brackets in order to more easily discern their placement.
<div class="inh1" style="outline-width: inherit;">
[div.inh1] This DIV should have an outline width of 1px when it is in focus, as it has a style attribute set to inherit the <code>outline-width</code> value. [/div.inh1]
</div>
<div class="inh2" style="outline-width: inherit;">
[div.inh2] This DIV should have an outline width of 1px when it is in focus, as it has a style attribute set to inherit the <code>outline-width</code> value. [/div.inh2]
</div>
This is the end of the parent DIV. [/div.parent]
</div><hr>
